 For this, having the right knowledge of makeup and applying it is also very important
 aise main ye jaruri he ki mechap applai karne se pehle aapako uske bare main kuch basic baaten pataa hon
 1
 powder kaa sahi istemalpowder lagane se mechap nikhar kar aata he lekin powder lagaate vakt is baat kaa dhyaan rakhana chahie ki ye puure chehre par baraabar laga ho

 2
 Concealer should be used carefully

 3
 Eye makeup To enhance the beauty of eyes, it is better to make eye makeup according to the trend
